# Project Dhruv Enhancement Plan with LangExtract and Milvus

## Understanding Confirmation
I confirm my understanding of the requirements based on the entire thread:
- **Core Objective**: Build an intelligent core engine for parsing OP Choudhary's X posts to extract and analyze context, sentiment, purpose, themes, locations, activities, tags, and descriptions. This engine must handle full tweet text, infer implicit elements (e.g., "‡§Æ‡§æ‡§§‡§æ‡§ì‡§Ç-‡§¨‡§π‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•ã" ‚Üí "‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§∂‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§ï‡§∞‡§£" as theme/purpose = "promote welfare"), and support the dashboard's "‡§ï‡§¨", "‡§ï‡§π‡§æ‡§Å", "‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ", "‡§ï‡•å‡§®/‡§ü‡•à‡§ó", "‡§ï‡•à‡§∏‡•á" fields with high completeness (aim <5% blanks).
- **Incorporating LangExtract and Milvus**: Use LangExtract for precise, grounded extraction (entities with character offsets, long-context handling via chunking/multiple passes). Use Milvus for hybrid storage/search (vector embeddings for semantic retrieval + metadata filtering for precise queries, e.g., search "‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§£" to find related posts).
- **Separate PR Branch**: Develop and test the engine in a separate branch (e.g., `feature/langextract-milvus-engine`). Validate with TDD, CI gates (coverage 95/70, security/performance/accessibility checks), and Vercel deployments. Integrate into main only after success (e.g., 90% accuracy on test dataset).
- **ML Training**: Use the 271 posts JSON as base dataset for labeling/training a custom model (e.g., IndicBERT fine-tuned for classification of context/sentiment/purpose).
- **Holistic Approach**: The plan covers everything in one markdown: overall plan/approach, 271 posts JSON (extended/simulated based on patterns from fetched data), prompt for atomic tasks, and detailed atomic tasks with TDD/GH actions.
- **No Mixing**: Engine tested separately; main dashboard remains unchanged until merge.

## Plan and Approach
### Overall Plan
The enhancement transforms the basic rule-based parsing into an LLM-powered, ML-augmented system using LangExtract (for structured extraction) and Milvus (for vector database storage/search). This addresses gaps like missing values in the dashboard PDF (e.g., blanks in "‡§ï‡§π‡§æ‡§Å"/"‡§ï‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ") and enables intelligent features (context inference, sentiment, purpose detection).

- **Phases**:
  1. **Data Preparation**: Use the 271 posts JSON as input. Auto-label with LangExtract for training data.
  2. **Extraction with LangExtract**: Define prompts for extracting entities (e.g., schemes, events, inferred tags like "#‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡§æ‡§®" from "‡§ï‡§ø‡§∏‡§æ‡§®‡•ã‡§Ç ‡§ï‡•á ‡§∏‡§æ‡§•") with offsets for grounding.
  3. **Storage and Search with Milvus**: Store parsed data as vectors + metadata in Milvus for hybrid queries (semantic + filtered, e.g., "‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§∂‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§ï‡§∞‡§£" search returning posts with inferred themes).
  4. **ML Training**: Fine-tune IndicBERT on labeled data for classification (context/themes, sentiment, purpose). Use for inference on new posts.
  5. **Integration**: Flask API endpoints for parsing/querying; Next.js dashboard consumes API for dynamic updates.
  6. **Testing/Deployment**: Separate branch for engine; CI with TDD, gates (coverage, perf LCP <=2.5s, a11y), Vercel audits. Merge post-success.
- **Approach**:
  - **LangExtract Integration**: Use few-shot prompts with examples from OP tweets (e.g., "‡§Æ‡§π‡§§‡§æ‡§∞‡•Ä ‡§µ‡§Ç‡§¶‡§® ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ú‡§®‡§æ" post for scheme extraction). Chunk long tweets, parallel process for efficiency.
  - **Milvus Integration**: Create collection with schema (id, timestamp, content, embedding, parsed_metadata like "themes": ["‡§Æ‡§π‡§ø‡§≤‡§æ ‡§∏‡§∂‡§ï‡•ç‡§§‡§ø‡§ï‡§∞‡§£"]). Index for cosine similarity; hybrid search (e.g., filter by sentiment=positive, semantic match to "‡§ï‡§≤‡•ç‡§Ø‡§æ‡§£ ‡§Ø‡•ã‡§ú‡§®‡§æ").
  - **ML Component**: Train on 80% of 271 posts (labeled via LangExtract); validate on 20%. Tasks: multi-label classification for themes/purpose, 3-class sentiment.
  - **Holistic Enhancements**: Add sentiment (positive/negative/neutral), purpose (e.g., "wish", "promote", "condolence"), context summary. Reduce blanks via inference/web enrichment.
  - **Reversibility/Safety**: Flags for LangExtract (`FLAG_LANGEXTRACT='on'`), Milvus (`FLAG_MILVUS_SEARCH='on'`); rollback by toggling to rule-based.
  - **Tools/Dependencies**: Python (re, indic-nlp-library, pandas, torch, transformers for IndicBERT, langextract, pymilvus). No new installs; assume available.
  - **Timeline**: 4 weeks (Prep: Week 1, Extract/Store: Week 2, Train/Infer: Week 3, Test/Integrate: Week 4).
  - **Risks/Rollback**: Low risk (static data); rollback: Vercel rollback (<=10 min), flag off.

## Atomic Tasks Prompt
You are a DevOps Agent operating under the Ironclad DevOps Rulebook v2.1, tasked with implementing the enhanced core engine for Project Dhruv using LangExtract (for extraction) and Milvus (for hybrid search/storage). Create a separate PR branch `feature/langextract-milvus-engine` for testing. Use the 271 posts JSON as the dataset. Follow red-green-refactor TDD for each task, with GH actions checks in `.github/workflows/ironclad.yml`. Output in diff-like format with + for added lines.

Epics:
- E1: LangExtract Integration (prompts, extraction, grounding).
- E2: Milvus Setup (collection, indexing, hybrid search).
- E3: ML Training (dataset labeling, fine-tune IndicBERT for context/sentiment/purpose).
- E4: Flask API Wiring (endpoints for parse/query).
- E5: Dashboard Integration (Next.js updates to consume API).
- E6: Validation and Audits (TDD, CI, Vercel).

Generate comprehensive atomic tasks (100+) with details: Task ID/Title, Acceptance Criteria, Test Plan (Red), Implementation Plan (Green), Refinement Scope (Refactor), Deliverables, GH Actions Check (e.g., coverage gate).

## Comprehensive Atomic Tasks
- Task ID: LE-01
  - Title: Setup LangExtract dependency
  - Acceptance Criteria: Library installed, basic extraction works on sample post.

  - Implementation Plan (Green): Add to requirements.txt; import in parser.py.
  - Refinement Scope (Refactor): Add version pin.
  - Deliverables: requirements.txt update.
  - GH Actions Check: lint-type, unit-tests, coverage-gate.
